Simply upload your files to a designated folder in your Cloud Storage bucket, and the extension will automatically process them and import the data into your specified Firestore collection.\n\n## How it works\n\n1. You upload JSON or CSV files to a specified folder in your default Cloud Storage bucket.\n2. The extension detects the new file and processes it based on its format:\n   - **JSON files**: The extension parses the JSON and imports it into Firestore.\n   - **CSV files**: The extension converts the CSV to JSON (using the first row as field names) and imports it into Firestore.\n3. The data is written to your specified Firestore collection using efficient batch operations.\n\n## Use cases\n\n- Migrate data from legacy systems to Firestore\n- Bulk import user data\n- Import product catalogs\n- Load test data for development and testing\n- Periodically update Firestore collections from external data sources\n\n## Additional setup\n\nBefore installing this extension, make sure you have:\n\n1. [Set up a Cloud Firestore database](https://firebase.google.com/docs/firestore/quickstart) in your Firebase project.\n2. [Set up Cloud Storage](https://firebase.google.com/docs/storage) in your Firebase project.\n\n## Billing\n\nThis extension uses the following Firebase services which may have associated charges:\n\n- Cloud Firestore\n- Cloud Storage\n- Cloud Functions\n\nThis extension also uses the following Firebase resources:\n\n- Cloud Storage Triggers\n\n## Best practices\n\n- For large datasets, consider splitting your data into multiple smaller files to improve processing efficiency.\n- Make sure your JSON or CSV files are well-formed and contain valid data.\n- For CSV files, ensure the first row contains the field names you want to use in Firestore.\n- For JSON files, structure your data in a way that matches how you want it stored in Firestore.\n","postinstallContent":"# Using the Firestore Importer Extension\n\nYou've successfully installed the Firestore Importer extension! Now you can easily import data from JSON and CSV files into your Firestore database.\n\n## Getting Started\n\nTo use this extension, follow these simple steps:\n\n1. **Upload your data files** to the `${param:IMPORT_FOLDER}` folder in your default Cloud Storage bucket.\n\n   - You can do this through the Firebase Console, Firebase Storage SDK, or the Google Cloud Console.\n   - Make sure your files have either a `.json` or `.csv` extension.\n\n2. **Wait for processing** - The extension will automatically detect the new file and begin processing it.\n\n   - The processing time depends on the size of your file and the complexity of the data.\n   - You can monitor the progress in the Firebase Functions logs.\n\n3. **Check your Firestore collection** - Once processing is complete, your data will be available in the `${param:TARGET_COLLECTION}` collection in Firestore.\n\n## File Format Requirements\n\n### JSON Files\n\nThe extension supports two JSON formats:\n\n1. **JSON Array**: An array of objects, where each object becomes a document in Firestore.\n\n   ```json\n   [\n     { \"name\": \"John\", \"age\": 30 },\n     { \"name\": \"Jane\", \"age\": 25 }\n   ]\n   ```\n\n2. **JSON Object**: An object with keys, where each key-value pair is processed based on its structure:\n   - If the value is an object, it becomes a document with the key as its ID.\n   - If the value is a primitive, it becomes a document with a field named after the key.\n   ```json\n   {\n     \"user1\": { \"name\": \"John\", \"age\": 30 },\n     \"user2\": { \"name\": \"Jane\", \"age\": 25 }\n   }\n   ```\n\n### CSV Files\n\nCSV files should have:\n\n- The first row containing column headers (these will be used as field names in Firestore)\n- Properly formatted CSV data in subsequent rows\n- Each row will become a document in Firestore\n\nExample:\n\n```\nname,age,email\nJohn,30,john@example.com\nJane,25,jane@example.com\n```\n\n## Data Type Handling\n\nThe extension automatically converts values to appropriate Firestore data types:\n\n- **CSV Files**:\n\n  - Numbers are converted to integers or floats\n  - \"true\" and \"false\" strings are converted to booleans\n  - Empty strings are converted to null\n\n- **JSON Files**:\n  - Data types are preserved as specified in the JSON\n\n## Monitoring & Troubleshooting\n\nYou can monitor the extension's activity in the Firebase Console:\n\n1. +/**
+ * Helper para obtener fechas formateadas
+ */
+function getFormattedScheduledTime(orderData) {
+    let scheduledTimeStr = 'Inmediato';
+    let scheduledDateTimeStr = 'Inmediato';
+    let timingType = 'Inmediato';
+
+    if (orderData.timing?.type === 'scheduled') {
+        const scheduledTime = orderData.timing.scheduledTime || '';
+        timingType = 'Programado';
+        scheduledTimeStr = scheduledTime;
+        scheduledDateTimeStr = scheduledTime;
+
+        // Intentar parsear la fecha programada
+        let dateObj = null;
+        if (orderData.timing.scheduledDate) {
+            const sd = orderData.timing.scheduledDate;
+            // Manejar Timestamp de Firestore (objeto con seconds) o Date nativo
+            if (sd.toDate && typeof sd.toDate === 'function') {
+                dateObj = sd.toDate();
+            } else if (sd.seconds) {
+                dateObj = new Date(sd.seconds * 1000);
+            } else if (sd._seconds) {
+                dateObj = new Date(sd._seconds * 1000);
+            } else {
+                dateObj = new Date(sd);
+            }
+        }
+
+        if (dateObj && !isNaN(dateObj.getTime())) {
+            // Configuraci├│n para Zona Horaria de Ecuador
+            const timeZone = 'America/Guayaquil';
+            const now = new Date();
+
+            // Formateadores
+            const isoDateFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('en-CA', { timeZone, year: 'numeric', month: '2-digit', day: '2-digit' });
+
+            const todayStr = isoDateFormatter.format(now);
+            const scheduledStr = isoDateFormatter.format(dateObj);
+
+            // Calcular ma├▒ana
+            const tomorrow = new Date(now);
+            tomorrow.setDate(tomorrow.getDate() + 1);
+            const tomorrowStr = isoDateFormatter.format(tomorrow);
+
+            if (scheduledStr === todayStr) {
+                scheduledDateTimeStr = `Hoy a las ${scheduledTime}`;
+            } else if (scheduledStr === tomorrowStr) {
+                scheduledDateTimeStr = `Ma├▒ana a las ${scheduledTime}`;
+            } else {
+                // Formato: "S├íbado 21 de febrero"
+                const fullDateFormatter = new Intl.DateTimeFormat('es-EC', {
+                    timeZone,
+                    weekday: 'long',
+                    day: 'numeric',
+                    month: 'long'
+                });
+
+                let datePart = fullDateFormatter.format(dateObj);
+                // Capitalizar primera letra
+                datePart = datePart.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + datePart.slice(1);
+
+                scheduledDateTimeStr = `${datePart} a las ${scheduledTime}`;
+            }
+        }
+    }
+
+    return { scheduledTimeStr, scheduledDateTimeStr, timingType };
+}

+const admin = require('firebase-admin');
+
+// Initialize the app with the service account from the emulator or just initializeApp if running locally with emulator
+admin.initializeApp({
+    projectId: 'fuddiverso'
+});
+const db = admin.firestore();
+
+async function run() {
+    const snaps = await db.collection('telegramTemplates').get();
+    snaps.forEach(doc => {
+        console.log("=== " + doc.id + " ===");
+        console.log(doc.data().template);
+    });
+}
+run().catch(console.error);
